I.
Oceanus
Sometimes
I
stand
upon
the
shore
Where
ocean
vaults
their
effluence
pour,
And
troubled
waters
sigh
and
shriek
Of
secrets
that
they
dare
not
speak.
nameless
valleys
far
below,
hills
plains
no
man
may
know,
The
mystic
swells
sullen
surges
Hint
like
accursed
thaumaturges
thousand
horrors,
big
with
awe,
That
forgotten
ages
saw.
O
salt,
salt
winds,
bleakly
sweep
Across
barren
heaving
deep;
wild,
wan
waves,
call
to
mind
chaos
Earth
hath
left
behind;
you
ask
one
thing
alone--
Leave,
leave
your
ancient
lore
unknown!
II.
Clouds
late
climb'd
a
lonely
height
watch'd
moon-streak'd
clouds
in
flight,
Whose
forms
fantastic
reel'd
whirl'd
Like
genii
spectral
world.
Thin
cirri
veil'd
silv'ry
dome
waver'd
foam,
While
shapes
darker,
heavier
kind
Scudded
before
daemon
wind.
Methought
churning
vapours
took
Now
anon
fearsome
look,
As
if
amidst
fog
blur
March'd
figures
known
sinister.
west
east
things
advanc'd--
mocking
train
leap'd
danc'd
Bacchanals
joined
hands
In
endless
file
thro'
airy
lands.
Aerial
mutt'rings,
dimly
heard,
comfort
my
spirit
stirr'd
With
hideous
thoughts,
bade
me
screen
My
sight
form
portentous
scene.
"Yon
fleeing
mists,"
murmurs
said,
"Are
ghosts
hopes,
deny'd
dead."
III.
Mother
One
night
wander'd
down
bank
deep
valley,
hush'd
dank,
stagnant
air
possess'd
taint
chill
made
sick
faint.
frequent
trees
on
ev'ry
hand
Loom'd
ghastly
goblin
band,
branches
`gainst
narrowing
sky
Took
fear'd--I
knew
why.
Deeper
plung'd,
seem'd
grope
For
some
lost
as
joy
or
hope,
Yet
found,
for
all
searchings
there,
Naught
save
phantoms
despair.
walls
contracted
went
Still
farther
mad
descent,
Till
soon,
moon
stars
bereft,
crouch'd
within
rocky
cleft
So
stone
Breath'd
primordial
unknown.
hands,
exploring,
strove
trace
features
valley's
face,
When
midst
gloom
find
An
outline
frightful
mind.
Not
any
shape
straining
eyes,
Could
have
seen,
might
recognize;
what
touch'd
bespoke
day
Too
old
man's
fugacious
sway.
clinging
lichens
moist
hoary
Forbade
read
antique
story;
But
hidden
water,
trickling
low,
Whisper'd
tales
should
know.
"Mortal,
ephemeral
bold,
mercy
keep
told,
think
sometimes
been,
sights
these
crumbling
rocks
seen;
sentience
ere
thy
weak
brook
Appear'd
lesser
magnitude,
living
yet
servive,
Tho'
human
ken
alive.
AM
THE
VOICE
OF
MOTHER
EARTH,
FORM
WHENCE
ALL
HORRORS
HAVE
THEIR
BIRTH."

England!
surging
sea
lies
between
tear
heart
thee?
Can
distant
birth
dwelling
drain
Th'
ancestral
blood
warms
loyal
vein?
Isle
Fathers!
hear
filial
song
sources
thee
belong!
World-Conquering
Mother!
mighty
Was
carv'd
savage
wilds
land:
Thy
matchless
sons
firm
foundation
laid;
arts
nascent
nation
made:
laws
republic
grew,
through
greatness,
kindred
greatness
knew.
springs
untainted
line
sees
Columbia's
virtues
thine?
Whilst
multitudes
dim
corners
creation
mongrel
slaves
crawl
hither
partake
Saxon
liberty
could
make,
alien
crew
grief
turn,
mother's
voice
Britain
burn.
aught
remove
cherish'd
chain
binds
blest
domain?
Revolution's
bitter

sway
soul
ties
race
obey?
Columbia
ye
will,
flesh
Britannic
still!
Hail!
oaken
shades,
meads
dewy
green,
oft
sleep,
ne'er
waking
seen.
Peal
out,
chimes,
vine-clad
tower
pray'd
fathers
vanish'd
hour:
countless
rev'rence
claim
bygone
worshippers
bore
name!
Their
around,
across
sea,
dream
sound.
Return,
Sweet
Vision!
Let
glimpse
again
stone-built
abbey,
rising
o'er
plain;
neighb'ring
village
sun-shower'd
square;
shaded
mill-stream,
forest
fair,
hedge-lin'd
lane,
leads
rustic
cot
sweet
contentment
peasant's
lot:
grove,
Druid
wraiths
possess'd,
flow'ring
fields,
fairy-castles
blest:
manor-house,
sedate
dark,
Set
shadows
wooded
park.
dreaming?
Must
eyelids
close
catch
fragrance
rose?
Is
fancy

vale
Thrills
warblings
nightingale?
golden

England's
fairies
trip
fields.
Old
love
No
mine,
blessed
memory;
Such
haunting
images
fires
Course
bounding
British
sires:
bodies,

souls

draw

Awake,
Columbia!
scorn

age

wide
Atlantic's
wildest
wave
Burst

fav'ring
Nature

Connecting

Our

one!
